First order principles are simply enough applied to all people in all places in all times.  Did you ever have people come in and they'll tell you  Doc, I've been everywhere and they tell me my blood work looks great.

These labs look awful. You see those people as well too. Right, so these things are not first order principles. Right. They do not apply to all people, in all places, in all times. Because we go from things, if you look at the course of history, of how this has moved out,  it's very interesting, because we all started out with the anatomical paradigm of disease, which basically says organs control disease, organs cause disease.

So, if I have a headache, like I did as a kid, it's a natural ideology that they're going to run and they're going to look at my brain.
